<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
O usuário inicialmente solicitou a criação de um clone do Uber, chamado Tuendi, para ser integrado a um aplicativo existente chamado TudoAqui. A solicitação evoluiu para uma reformulação e expansão completa do aplicativo TudoAqui, incluindo:
1.  **Funcionalidades Principais**: Substituição do módulo de Táxi pelo Tuendi, um sistema robusto de autenticação com papéis (roles), uma carteira digital unificada, sistema de pontos, chat em tempo real e notificações.
2.  **Funcionalidades de Engajamento**: Um sistema de streak diário por login, um sistema de cupons de desconto e a capacidade de exportar relatórios de transações.
3.  **Funcionalidades de Negócio**: Um gateway de pagamento (simulado) para recarregar a carteira, e uma apresentação de projeto profissional (pitch deck) para captação de recursos.
4.  **Presença Online**: Criação de um site público (landing page) para o projeto, com um script de implantação para um servidor web.
5.  **Expansão de Plataforma**: A conversão do aplicativo web em aplicativos móveis nativos para iOS e Android.

**User's preferred language**: Portuguese (Português)

**what currently exists?**
O agente implementou com sucesso a grande maioria das funcionalidades solicitadas. O aplicativo TudoAqui é agora uma super app funcional com múltiplos módulos integrados.
-   **Backend**: Foram criados e integrados módulos para  (autenticação com JWT e papéis),  (carteira e pontos),  (corridas), , ,  (gateway simulado), ,  (sequência de login) e  (exportação CSV). A interatividade entre módulos está funcionando (ex: corridas concluídas geram pontos na carteira).
-   **Frontend**: A UI foi completamente modernizada. Existem páginas funcionais para Login, Perfil de Usuário, Dashboard (com UI baseada em papéis), Tuendi (solicitação de corrida), Carteira, Cupons, Pagamentos, Relatórios e uma página de apresentação interativa (). Uma nova  também foi adicionada ao app React.
-   **Site Estático**: Um diretório separado  foi criado, contendo um site HTML estático completo e um script  para fácil implantação.

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()

        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/auth/me', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/me': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/me?
